    <section class="layout__item directions svelte-1dqq0pw">
        <div class="heading svelte-1dqq0pw">
            <h2 id="directions" class="directions__title svelte-1dqq0pw">directions</h2>
        </div>
        <ul class="direction-list svelte-1dqq0pw">
            <li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Whisk flour, sugar, baking powder, spices and salt in a bowl.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">In a separate bowl whisk together milk, pumpkin, melted butter, and egg.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Fold mixture into dry ingredients.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Spray or grease a skillet and heat over medium heat: pour in 1/4 cup batter for each pancake.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Cook pancakes about 3 minutes per side. Serve with butter and syrup.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Makes about six 6-inch pancakes.</li>
        </ul>

                                                <div title="" class="text-truncate truncate truncate-ready post__text-truncate--flex">
                                                    <span class="text-truncate__text paragraph">This batter is very thick but it is better this way. I also use almond milk along with vegan butter and it is always more difficult to &amp;quot;feel&amp;quot; like the food is cooked through because almond milk doesn't respond the same way as regular milk. And then if you added &amp;quot;more&amp;quot; almond milk then it was definitely not going to seem cooked all of the way. I make this recipe and it was perfect. You just have to go in with the realization that you will have a much more moist/doughy product at the end with almond milk of anything you bake.</span>

          <div class="post__text svelte-omstw2">
              

<div title="These pancakes were a real hit at my house!  All of my children loved them.  I made a double recipe and ended up with some left over.  Suffice it to say, they freeze and reheat in the toaster nicely.   Just remember to put wax paper between them so they don't stick together. Also, if you are curious, 6 tbs. of pumpkin puree is about 1/3 of a can. Lastly, the batter is a little thick.  If you like a little thinner batter and pancake, plan to add a little extra milk. Thanks for a great recipe!!!" class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         These pancakes were a real hit at my house!  All of my children loved them.  I made a double recipe and ended up with some left over.  Suffice it to say, they freeze and reheat in the toaster nicely.   Just remember to put wax paper between them so they don't stick together. Also, if you are curious, 6 tbs. of pumpkin puree is about 1/3 of a can. Lastly, the batter is a little thick.  If you like a little thinner batter and pancake, plan to add a little extra milk. Thanks for a great recipe!!!
    </div>

<div title="Where's the 10-star button???!!!  I ADORE pumpkin.  My grandmother used to bring 2 pumpkin pies to Thanksgiving:  one for the family, and one for me!  I bought a can of pure pumpkin specifically to make pumpkin pancakes.  While I was waiting for a morning that my husband was working so I could try them, I made #53751 (Pumpkin Butter), and #453580 (Pumpkin Grilled Cheese).  When I called my daughter and her friend to breakfast, my daughter growled, &quot;MOM!  How do you even know Danielle likes pumpkin!?&quot;  They sat at the table where I'd placed the pancakes, pumpkin butter, whipped cream, chocolate sprinkles and syrup.  Danielle took the teeniest bite in fear of hating them.  AND I QUOTE:  &quot;I think my mouth died and went to heaven&quot;, she said.  My daughter of course LOVED them as well!!! SUBSTITUTIONS:  I used 2 tsp of pumpkin pie spice instead (I keep it on hand for my recipe #452939), and used 3/4 cups flour and 1/2 cup whole wheat flour.  Used 2 tbsp applesauce in place of the butter, and based on reviews I used 1 1/4 cups milk to thin it out.  Also used 1tbsp of Splenda in place of the sugar.  Lastly, I used about 1/4 cup of pumpkin because, as I said, I LOVE PUMPKIN!  This is a definite keeper!  I can't wait for the family Christmas breakfast in our jammies with the whole family to show this one off!!!!!  Thank you thank you Hope!" class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         Where's the 10-star button???!!!  I ADORE pumpkin.  My grandmother used to bring 2 pumpkin pies to Thanksgiving:  one for the family, and one for me!  I bought a can of pure pumpkin specifically to make pumpkin pancakes.  While I was waiting for a morning that my husband was working so I could try them, I made #53751 (Pumpkin Butter), and #453580 (Pumpkin Grilled Cheese).  When I called my daughter and her friend to breakfast, my daughter growled, "MOM!  How do you even know Danielle likes pumpkin!?"  They sat at the table where I'd placed the pancakes, pumpkin butter, whipped cream, chocolate sprinkles and syrup.  Danielle took the teeniest bite in fear of hating them.  AND I QUOTE:  "I think my mouth died and went to heaven", she said.  My daughter of course LOVED them as well!!! SUBSTITUTIONS:  I used 2 tsp of pumpkin pie spice instead (I keep it on hand for my recipe #452939), and used 3/4 cups flour and 1/2 cup whole wheat flour.  Used 2 tbsp applesauce in place of the butter, and based on reviews I used 1 1/4 cups milk to thin it out.  Also used 1tbsp of Splenda in place of the sugar.  Lastly, I used about 1/4 cup of pumpkin because, as I said, I LOVE PUMPKIN!  This is a definite keeper!  I can't wait for the family Christmas breakfast in our jammies with the whole family to show this one off!!!!!  Thank you thank you Hope!

          <div class="post__text svelte-omstw2">
              

<div title="Excellent recipe! Only changes I made were to add more cinnamon and use brown sugar instead of white. I also let the batter rest a few minutes before using. The batter will be pretty thick, but will cook up fine. Used 1/4 cup measure as directed and my cakes cooked up in a little under 2 minutes per side on a 375 degree electric griddle. I didn't use any cooking spray since the griddle is nonstick. My yield was about 11 6&quot; cakes. These have a great flavor and are slightly denser than regular pancakes, but are by far the fluffiest pumpkin ones I've ever had! Served with butter, syrup, and candied pecans." class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         Excellent recipe! Only changes I made were to add more cinnamon and use brown sugar instead of white. I also let the batter rest a few minutes before using. The batter will be pretty thick, but will cook up fine. Used 1/4 cup measure as directed and my cakes cooked up in a little under 2 minutes per side on a 375 degree electric griddle. I didn't use any cooking spray since the griddle is nonstick. My yield was about 11 6" cakes. These have a great flavor and are slightly denser than regular pancakes, but are by far the fluffiest pumpkin ones I've ever had! Served with butter, syrup, and candied pecans.
    </div>

          <div class="post__text svelte-omstw2">
              

<div title="I did two things differently with this recipe.  I substituted 1/2 tsp of baking soda and 1 1/2 tsp of baking powder instead of all baking powder.  I read somewhere that baking soda helps with browning.  I also toasted the spices in a dry skillet before adding them to bloom them.  Fantastic spicy flavor and super light and fluffy, they were like cake versions of pumpkin pie.  Lovely!" class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         I did two things differently with this recipe.  I substituted 1/2 tsp of baking soda and 1 1/2 tsp of baking powder instead of all baking powder.  I read somewhere that baking soda helps with browning.  I also toasted the spices in a dry skillet before adding them to bloom them.  Fantastic spicy flavor and super light and fluffy, they were like cake versions of pumpkin pie.  Lovely!
    </div>

<div title="Where's the 10-star button???!!!  I ADORE pumpkin.  My grandmother used to bring 2 pumpkin pies to Thanksgiving:  one for the family, and one for me!  I bought a can of pure pumpkin specifically to make pumpkin pancakes.  While I was waiting for a morning that my husband was working so I could try them, I made #53751 (Pumpkin Butter), and #453580 (Pumpkin Grilled Cheese).  When I called my daughter and her friend to breakfast, my daughter growled, &quot;MOM!  How do you even know Danielle likes pumpkin!?&quot;  They sat at the table where I'd placed the pancakes, pumpkin butter, whipped cream, chocolate sprinkles and syrup.  Danielle took the teeniest bite in fear of hating them.  AND I QUOTE:  &quot;I think my mouth died and went to heaven&quot;, she said.  My daughter of course LOVED them as well!!! SUBSTITUTIONS:  I used 2 tsp of pumpkin pie spice instead (I keep it on hand for my recipe #452939), and used 3/4 cups flour and 1/2 cup whole wheat flour.  Used 2 tbsp applesauce in place of the butter, and based on reviews I used 1 1/4 cups milk to thin it out.  Also used 1tbsp of Splenda in place of the sugar.  Lastly, I used about 1/4 cup of pumpkin because, as I said, I LOVE PUMPKIN!  This is a definite keeper!  I can't wait for the family Christmas breakfast in our jammies with the whole family to show this one off!!!!!  Thank you thank you Hope!" class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         Where's the 10-star button???!!!  I ADORE pumpkin.  My grandmother used to bring 2 pumpkin pies to Thanksgiving:  one for the family, and one for me!  I bought a can of pure pumpkin specifically to make pumpkin pancakes.  While I was waiting for a morning that my husband was working so I could try them, I made #53751 (Pumpkin Butter), and #453580 (Pumpkin Grilled Cheese).  When I called my daughter and her friend to breakfast, my daughter growled, "MOM!  How do you even know Danielle likes pumpkin!?"  They sat at the table where I'd placed the pancakes, pumpkin butter, whipped cream, chocolate sprinkles and syrup.  Danielle took the teeniest bite in fear of hating them.  AND I QUOTE:  "I think my mouth died and went to heaven", she said.  My daughter of course LOVED them as well!!! SUBSTITUTIONS:  I used 2 tsp of pumpkin pie spice instead (I keep it on hand for my recipe #452939), and used 3/4 cups flour and 1/2 cup whole wheat flour.  Used 2 tbsp applesauce in place of the butter, and based on reviews I used 1 1/4 cups milk to thin it out.  Also used 1tbsp of Splenda in place of the sugar.  Lastly, I used about 1/4 cup of pumpkin because, as I said, I LOVE PUMPKIN!  This is a definite keeper!  I can't wait for the family Christmas breakfast in our jammies with the whole family to show this one off!!!!!  Thank you thank you Hope!

    <section class="layout__item directions svelte-1dqq0pw">
        <div class="heading svelte-1dqq0pw">
            <h2 class="directions__title svelte-1dqq0pw">directions</h2>
        </div>
        <ul class="direction-list svelte-1dqq0pw">
            <li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">In a large bowl add the flour, spices and baking powder.  Use a whisk to airate it and get lots of air inches.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">In a seperate bowl, beat the eggs with a beater until foamy - about 3 minutes.  Add the yoghurt, milk, pumpkin, vanilla, sugar, and brown sugar.  Beat to mix well.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Pour the egg mix into the flour mix and gently fold to combine.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Spoon 1/4 of a cup on to a buttered hot pan and cook over a medium heat.</li><li class="direction svelte-1dqq0pw">Let each side cook for about 3 minutes.</li>
        </ul>

<div title="Wonderful flavored pancakes and nice switch!!!  I made 1/2 of the recipe and followed as written and they were nice and fluffy and moist.  We tried them with some butter and a shake of powdered sugar, but not sweet enough for our tastes.  We then tried sprinkling on a cinnamon/sugar mixture which went perfectly with these cakes.  I also think maple syrup would be good too!!!  Thanks for sharing the recipe.  Made for ZWT8." class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         Wonderful flavored pancakes and nice switch!!!  I made 1/2 of the recipe and followed as written and they were nice and fluffy and moist.  We tried them with some butter and a shake of powdered sugar, but not sweet enough for our tastes.  We then tried sprinkling on a cinnamon/sugar mixture which went perfectly with these cakes.  I also think maple syrup would be good too!!!  Thanks for sharing the recipe.  Made for ZWT8.

<div title="This recipe did not work out for me.  Maybe it was because I used AP flour, and Greek yogurt, as those were what I had on hand.  The batter was super thick, and the pancakes were super dense, did not fluff up at all, and even with 8 minutes on each side, didn't really get done.  The taste was great, but consistency was way off." class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         This recipe did not work out for me.  Maybe it was because I used AP flour, and Greek yogurt, as those were what I had on hand.  The batter was super thick, and the pancakes were super dense, did not fluff up at all, and even with 8 minutes on each side, didn't really get done.  The taste was great, but consistency was way off.
    </div>

<div title="<p><img src=http://i80.photobucket.com/albums/j166/ZaarNicksMom/PACsticker-Adopted.jpg alt=/ /> <br /><br />As a toddler, my nic-name was Pompom (my Poppy had a golf hat with a pompom and it was one of my first words, and it stuck as my nic name). &amp;nbsp;My Poppy has long since passed, but I fondly remember him every time I log on. &amp;nbsp;I'm a stay at home mum of four aged: 10, 8, 7 and almost 6. I have a severe egg allergy and am lactose intolerant, I&amp;nbsp;enjoy working out ways to still enjoy food minus eggs and milk. I have been married for 14 years and have one very happy and well fed hubby.<br />My goal is to try one new recipe a week, for the past 8 years have achieved this. &amp;nbsp;I own over 300 cookbooks, but no longer purchase them - but regularly print out recipes to try later.<br />When I am not cooking, I am busy household of 6 and going to the gym (to work off the wonderful calories I consumed the day before) and helping at school and church.<br />My philosophy in life is: as we have to eat, we may as well eat well.</p>" class="text-truncate svelte-1aswkii">

    <div class="text svelte-1aswkii truncated">
         &lt;p&gt;&lt;img src=http://i80.photobucket.com/albums/j166/ZaarNicksMom/PACsticker-Adopted.jpg alt=/ /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;As a toddler, my nic-name was Pompom (my Poppy had a golf hat with a pompom and it was one of my first words, and it stuck as my nic name). &amp;nbsp;My Poppy has long since passed, but I fondly remember him every time I log on. &amp;nbsp;I'm a stay at home mum of four aged: 10, 8, 7 and almost 6. I have a severe egg allergy and am lactose intolerant, I&amp;nbsp;enjoy working out ways to still enjoy food minus eggs and milk. I have been married for 14 years and have one very happy and well fed hubby.&lt;br /&gt;My goal is to try one new recipe a week, for the past 8 years have achieved this. &amp;nbsp;I own over 300 cookbooks, but no longer purchase them - but regularly print out recipes to try later.&lt;br /&gt;When I am not cooking, I am busy household of 6 and going to the gym (to work off the wonderful calories I consumed the day before) and helping at school and church.&lt;br /&gt;My philosophy in life is: as we have to eat, we may as well eat well.&lt;/p&gt;

        // OrigPubDate modification logic
        cleanOrigPubDate = function s_cleanOrigPubDate() {
            var opd = mdManager.getParameterString("OrigPubDate"),
                opd_array = [],
                opd_days = 0,
                opd_string = "",
                orig_date,
                mod_date;
            try {
                if (opd && typeof opd === "string") {
                    opd_array = opd.match(/\d\d\d\d-\d\d-\d\d/g);
                    opd_string = opd_array ? opd_array.join("|") : "";
                    if (opd_string !== "") {
                        if (opd_array[0]) {
                            orig_date = new Date(opd_array[0]);
                            opd_string += "|" + dateDeltas(orig_date);
                        }
                        if (opd_array[1]) {
                            mod_date = new Date(opd_array[1]);
                            opd_string += "|" + dateDeltas(mod_date);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                //  something went wrong
            }
            return opd_string;
        }
        dateDeltas = function s_dateDeltas(dateObj) {
            var today = new Date(),
                days = Math.floor(Math.abs(today.getTime() - dateObj.getTime()) / (1000 * 3600 * 24));
            if (days < 8) {
                return (days + (days === 1 ? " day" : " days"));
            } else if (days > 7 && days < 31) {
                return ("8 days-1 month");
            } else if (days > 30 && days < 366) {
                return (Math.floor(days / 30.417) + "-" + Math.ceil(days / 30.417) + " months");
            } else if (days > 365) {
                return ">1 year";
            }
        }

        origVars = s.linkTrackVars;
        s.linkTrackVars = "";
        for (var key in options) {
            s.contextData[key] = options[key].toString().replace(/https?:\/\/([^.]*).*.com\/?/, "$1.../");
            s.linkTrackVars += ",contextData." + key;
            _satellite.logger.log(key.toString() + ":" + s.contextData[key], 1);
        }
        // Add custom event
        s.contextData["eventModuleLinkClick"] = "1";
        s.linkTrackVars += ",contextData.eventModuleLinkClick";
        // fire beacon
        _satellite.logger.log('Sending s.tl call from moduleTackLS.');
        s.tl(obj, 'o', options.ModuleName);
        // clear everything out
        for (var clearKey in options) {
            s.contextData[clearKey] = "";
        }
        s.contextData["eventModuleLinkClick"] = "";
        if (typeof s.events === "string") { s.events = s.events.replace(/event24,?/, ""); };
        s.linkTrackVars = origVars;
    }
};

// write an arbitrary set of analytics data to a 
// localStorage record call TRACKLSANALYTICS
if (SNI.Analytics.hasLocalStorage && typeof localStorage === "object") {
    SNI.Analytics.trackViaLS = function (opts) {
        var lsval = JSON.stringify(opts),
            retval;
        try {
            localStorage.setItem("TRACKLSANALYTICS", lsval);
            retval = true;
        } catch (e) {
            //console.log("couldn't write localStorage");
            retval = false;
        }
        return retval;
    };
}

SNI.Analytics.refreshContext = function refreshContext() {
    // OrigPubDate modification logic
    cleanOrigPubDate = function s_cleanOrigPubDate() {
        var opd = mdManager.getParameterString("OrigPubDate"),
            opd_array = [],
            opd_days = 0,
            opd_string = "",
            orig_date,
            mod_date;
        try {
            if (opd && typeof opd === "string") {
                opd_array = opd.match(/\d\d\d\d-\d\d-\d\d/g);
                opd_string = opd_array ? opd_array.join("|") : "";
                if (opd_string !== "") {
                    if (opd_array[0]) {
                        orig_date = new Date(opd_array[0]);
                        opd_string += "|" + dateDeltas(orig_date);
                    }
                    if (opd_array[1]) {
                        mod_date = new Date(opd_array[1]);
                        opd_string += "|" + dateDeltas(mod_date);
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
            //  something went wrong
        }
        return opd_string;
    }
    dateDeltas = function s_dateDeltas(dateObj) {
        var today = new Date(),
            days = Math.floor(Math.abs(today.getTime() - dateObj.getTime()) / (1000 * 3600 * 24));
        if (days < 8) {
            return (days + (days === 1 ? " day" : " days"));
        } else if (days > 7 && days < 31) {
            return ("8 days-1 month");
        } else if (days > 30 && days < 366) {
            return (Math.floor(days / 30.417) + "-" + Math.ceil(days / 30.417) + " months");
        } else if (days > 365) {
            return ">1 year";
        }
    }

    // refresh context data
    var key,value,upperKey;
    for (key in mdManager.getKeys()) {
        value = mdManager.getParameter(key);
        upperKey = key.toString().toUpperCase();
        if (upperKey  !== "UNIQUEID") { value = value.toString().toLowerCase(); }

        // remap mdManager to appropriate contextData variables
		if (upperKey === "URL") { key = "pageName"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "TITLE") { key = "pageTitle"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "CATEGORYDSPNAME") { key = "contentSiteSection"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "SCTNDSPNAME") { key = "contentSubSection"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "SUBSECTION") { key = "contentSubSection2"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "SUBSECTIONL2") { key = "contentSubSection3"; } // verify key is correct format and if this is being used at all
		else if (upperKey  === "TYPE") { key = "contentPageType"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "UNIQUEID") { key = "pageUniqueID"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "DELIVERY_CHANNEL") { key = "deliveryChannel"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "IMGURL") { key = "imageURL"; }
        else if (upperKey  === "ORIGPUBDATE") {
            s.contextData["originalPublishDate"] = mdManager.getParameter(key).split("|")[0];
            s.contextData["latestPublishDate"] = mdManager.getParameter(key).split("|")[1];
            value = cleanOrigPubDate();
        }
        else if (upperKey  === "SHOW_ABBR") { key = "showName"; }
        else if (upperKey  === "POINTOFINTEREST") { key="poi"; }
        else if (upperKey  === "FILTER") { key = "searchFilters"; }
        else if (upperKey  === "SEARCHTERMS") { key = "searchTermContextual"; }
        else if (upperKey  === "DIMENSIONS") { key = "searchDimensions"; }
        else if (upperKey  === "DIMENSIONVALUES") { key = "searchDimensionValues"; }
        else if (upperKey  === "NOSEARCHRESULTS") { key = "noResultsSearchTerm"; }
		else if (upperKey  === "TAGGROUP1") { key = "contentTags"; }
      

        delete s.contextData[key];
        s.contextData[key] = value;
    }	
  
   // adding platform logic
    s.contextData.platform ='web';
  
  // thirdparty flag change
 try {
     var thirdpartytag='false';  
   if (!! _satellite.getVar('optanonconsent') &&_satellite.getVar('optanonconsent').indexOf('C0004:0') > -1){     
     thirdpartytag = "true";
       }
     // adding privacy logic
          s.contextData['opt.dmp']='Y';
          s.contextData['opt.sell']='Y'; 
          s.contextData['cm.ssf']='';
      if(thirdpartytag === "true") {  
          s.contextData['cm.ssf']='1' ;                  
          s.contextData['opt.dmp']='N' ;
          s.contextData['opt.sell']='N' ;
      }
       } catch (e) {

      }
    // content tags and s.products
    setContentTagsFromHeaders = function conTagFromH (tagHeaders) {
        if ( !Array.isArray(tagHeaders) ) { return false; };
        s.contextData["contentTags"] = "";
        var tagArray = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < tagHeaders.length; i++) {
            var currentHeader = tagHeaders[i];
            var tagItem = currentHeader + "|";
            if (mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader) != undefined) { tagItem += mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader) }
            tagArray.push(tagItem);
        }
        s.contextData["contentTags"] = tagArray.join().toLowerCase();
    };
    var tagHeaders = [],lowerCaseType;
    var fullURL = location.href;
    var domainRegex = /^https?\:\/\/(?:.*\.)?(?:([^\.]+)\.com).*$/;
    var domain = fullURL.match(domainRegex)[1];
    lowerCaseType = mdManager.getParameter("type").toString().toLowerCase();
    // collect tags and s.products under certain conditions
    if (lowerCaseType === "recipe" && (domain === "foodnetwork" || domain === "cookingchanneltv")) {
        tagHeaders = ["cuisine", "difficulty", "mainingredient", "mealpart", "preptime", "technique", "dish", "mealtype", "nutrition", "occasions", "courses", "taste"];
        setContentTagsFromHeaders(tagHeaders);
    } else if (lowerCaseType === "example_other_page_type" && domain === "someParticularSite") {
        tagHeaders = ["ex_tag_header_1", "ex_tag_header_2"];
        setContentTagsFromHeaders(tagHeaders);
    } else {
        // overwrite contentTags if any of the following are present
        if (sessionStorage.getItem("prodSetByShopTrack") != "true") {
            if (mdManager.getParameterString("Overlay_TagGroup1") != "") {
                s.contextData["contentTags"] = mdManager.getParameterString("Overlay_TagGroup1").replace(/;/g, "|");
            } else if (mdManager.getParameterString("TagGroup1") != "") {
                s.contextData["contentTags"] = mdManager.getParameterString("TagGroup1").replace(/;/g, "|");
            }
            // remove legacy wayfair stl from the photo tags/list2 meta-data
            if (s.contextData["contentTags"] && s.contextData["contentTags"].indexOf("wayfair/shop_this_look") != -1) {
                s.contextData["contentTags"] = s.contextData["contentTags"].replace("partner|wayfair/shop_this_look,", "");
            }
            if (mdManager.getParameterString("shopping").toString().toLowerCase() == "shopping") {
                if (mdManager.getParameter("products").indexOf("|") == -1) {
                    productList = mdManager.getParameter("products").replace(/,;/g, ",;s|na|");
                    s.products = ";s|na|" + productList;
                } else {
                    productList = mdManager.getParameter("products").replace(/,;/g, ",;s|");
                    s.products = ";s|" + productList;
                }
                s.products += ",;c|" + mdManager.getParameter("componentName");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("componentTitle");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("imageCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("productCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("visibleProductCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("perImageProductCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("productPosition");

                s.products = s.products.toLowerCase();
                s.contextData["shoppingProducts"] = "D=products";
                s.contextData["eventShoppingProductsImpressions"] = "1";
                s.events = s.apl(s.events, "prodView", ",", 2);
            
                //For Apple News shopping product clicks
                if (location.host.indexOf("click.tinysharks.") != -1 || location.host.indexOf("click.home.") != -1 || location.host.indexOf("click.fnr.") != -1) {
                    s.events = "scAdd";
                    s.contextData["eventShoppingProductsImpressions"] = "";
                    s.contextData["moduleName"] = mdManager.getParameter("componentName");
                    s.contextData["linkTitle"] = mdManager.getParameter("sourcePageTitle");
                    s.contextData["linkPosition"] = "apple news";
                    s.contextData["targetURL"] = location.host + location.pathname;
                    s.contextData["locURL"] = mdManager.getParameter("sourcePageUrl");
                }  
            }
            sessionStorage.setItem("prodSetByShopTrack", "false");
        }	
    }
}

SNI.Analytics.attachClickTracking = function sni_analytics_attachclicktracking(opts) {
    var $container = $(opts.selector);
    $(opts.selector).find("button,a").off('click.sni_analytics').on('click.sni_analytics', function () {
        SNI.Analytics.moduleTrackLS(this, {
            ModuleName: opts.namespace,
            LinkTitle: $(this).attr("title") ? $(this).attr("title") : $(this).html(),
            LinkPosition: $container.index(this),
            TargetUrl: $(this).attr("href") && $(this).attr("href")
        });
    });
    _satellite.logger.log("attachClickTracking: " + JSON.stringify(opts), 1);
};

$(function () {
    if (typeof s === "object") {
        s.trackModLocalStorage = function () {
            var modName, contextVars, i;
            try {
                if (localStorage.getItem("TRACKMOD")) {
                    modName = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("TRACKMOD")),
                        contextVars = Object.keys(modName).sort(),
                        i = contextVars.length || 0;
                    while (i--) {
                        s.contextData[contextVars[i]] = modName[contextVars[i]];
                    }
                    // s.events = s.apl(s.events, "event24", ",", 2);
                    s.contextData["eventModuleLinkClick"] = "1";
                    if (typeof s.Integrate === "object" && typeof s.Integrate.removeTrackMod !== "object") {
                        s.Integrate.add("removeTrackMod");
                        s.Integrate.removeTrackMod.useVars = function () {
                            _satellite.logger.log("DELETING TRACKMOD", 1);
                            localStorage.removeItem("TRACKMOD");
                        }
                    }
                    return true;
                }
            } catch (e) {
                // couldn't read localstorage
            }
        };
    }
});

    ) {
      _satellite.logger.warn(
        's.t() has been disabled on sites containing part of this path.'
      )
      return
    }
    // Code to run before old s.t() call
    s.contextData['eventPageConsumption'] = '1'
    s.contextData.serverCallType = 'pageview'
    s.contextData.platform = 'web'
    try {
      var thirdpartytag = 'false'

      if (
        !!_satellite.getVar('optanonconsent') &&
        _satellite.getVar('optanonconsent').indexOf('C0004:0') > -1
      ) {
        thirdpartytag = 'true'
      }
      // adding privacy logic
      s.contextData['opt.dmp'] = 'Y'
      s.contextData['opt.sell'] = 'Y'
      s.contextData['cm.ssf'] = ''
      if (thirdpartytag === 'true') {
        s.contextData['cm.ssf'] = '1'
        s.contextData['opt.dmp'] = 'N'
        s.contextData['opt.sell'] = 'N'
      }

      //privacy code end
      s.contextData['businessUnit'] = 'discovery digital studios'
      if (_satellite.getVar('Core:Constant:Analytics Code Version')) {
        s.contextData['analyticsCodeVersion'] = _satellite.getVar(
          'Core:Constant:Analytics Code Version'
        )
      }
      if (_satellite.getVar('Core:Constant:Distribution Product')) {
        s.contextData['productDetails'] = _satellite.getVar(
          'Core:Constant:Distribution Product'
        )
      }
      // old s.t() call as callback to refreshing context data
      refreshContextData(e, t, extra1, extra2, extra3, tempTrack)
      // Code to run after old s.t() call
      if (thirdpartytag === 'false') {
        runThirdPartyIntegrations()
      }
    } catch (err) {}
  }

  function runThirdPartyIntegrations () {
    _satellite.logger.info('Running Third Party Integrations')
    sendComscoreBeacon()
    sendGA_newBeacon()
    addGoogleTags()
    addFloodlightStuff()
    addPostUp_js()
    sendOtherFloodlightBeacons()
    sendDoubleClickBeacon()
  }

  function sendComscoreBeacon () {
    if (s.pe !== 'lnk_o' && s.contextData['serverCallType'] === 'pageview') {
      var ns__t = new Date().getTime(),
        cur_prot = window.location.protocol.toLowerCase(),
        cur_host = window.location.host.toLowerCase(),
        cur_path = window.location.pathname.toLowerCase()

      var path = 'https://sb.scorecardresearch.com/b'
      path += '?c1=2&c2=6035648&c3=&c4=&c5=&c6='
      path += '&c7=' + cur_prot + '//' + cur_host + cur_path
      path += '&c8=' + s.contextData['pageTitle']
      path += '&c9=' + encodeURI(s.referrer)
      path += '&c15=&ns__t=' + ns__t + '&ns_c=UTF-8'

      _satellite.logger.log('sending comscore beacon')
      var tempImg = new Image()
      tempImg.src = path
    }
  }


  function sendGA_newBeacon () {
    if (!s.pe && s.contextData['pageName']) {
      if (
        location.host.indexOf('golden.') == -1 &&
        location.host.indexOf('mynewsletters.') == -1
      ) {
        if (
          location.host.indexOf('.discovery.') != -1 ||
          location.pathname.indexOf('/discovery-com/') != -1
        ) {
          _satellite.logger.log('Adding GA')
          ;(function (i, s, o, g, r, a, m) {
            i['GoogleAnalyticsObject'] = r
            ;(i[r] =
              i[r] ||
              function () {
                ;(i[r].q = i[r].q || []).push(arguments)
              }),
              (i[r].l = 1 * new Date())
            ;(a = s.createElement(o)), (m = s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0])
            a.async = 1
            a.src = g
            m.parentNode.insertBefore(a, m)
          })(
            window,
            document,
            'script',
            'https://www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js',
            'ga'
          )

          ga('create', 'UA-43824761-30', 'auto')
          ga('send', 'pageview', {
            dimension5: _satellite.getVar('Show_Name'),
            dimension6: _satellite.getVar('Page_Type'),
            dimension24: 'non authenticated visit',
            dimension27: _satellite.getVar('Site_Name'),
            dimension28: 'web',
            dimension29: 'discovery-web'
          })

        }
      }
    }
  }

  function sendDoubleClickBeacon () {
    if (isHGTV) {
      if (typeof mdManager != 'undefined') {
        if (
          mdManager.getParameterString('Type').toLowerCase() ===
            'photogallerypage' &&
          mdManager.getParameterString('sponsorship').toLowerCase() ===
            'hg_pk_room_by_room'
        ) {
          _satellite.logger.log('Sending Double-Click Beacon.')
          ord = Math.random()
          ord = ord * 10000000000000000000
          pixel =
            '<IMG SRC="https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackimp/N5214.3192.HGTV/B21356059.224580597;dc_trk_aid=422881682;dc_trk_cid=103475023;ord=' +
            ord +
            ';dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=;tfua=?" WIDTH="1" HEIGHT="1" BORDER="0" ALT="Advertisement">'
          $(document.body).prepend(pixel)
        }
      }
    }
  }

var shopTrack = function (obj,shopping,componentName,componentTitle,partner,products,imageCount,productCount,visibleProductCount,perImageProductCount,productPosition,eventType) {
	_satellite.logger.log('Calling shopTrack Function'); 
  
  	var shopArgs = [].slice.call(arguments);
	_satellite.logger.log(shopArgs);
  
    sessionStorage.setItem("prodSetByShopTrack", "true");  // this will prevent the analytics doplugins code from overwriting products data set in this function
	s.trackExternalLinks=false;
	s.products="";
    s.contextData["shoppingProducts"] = "";
    // create products string
	if(products.indexOf("|") == -1) {
		productList=products.replace(/,;/g, ",;s|na|").replace(/&quot;/g, '\"').replace(/&amp;/g, '\&').replace(/&apos;/g, '\'');
        s.products =";s|na|" + productList;
	}
	else {
		productList=products.replace(/,;/g, ",;s|").replace(/&quot;/g, '\"').replace(/&amp;/g, '\&').replace(/&apos;/g, '\'');
		s.products =";s|" + productList;
    }
    s.products += ",;c|" + componentName;
    s.products += "|" + componentTitle;
    s.products += "|" + imageCount;
    s.products += "|" + productCount;
    s.products += "|" + visibleProductCount;
    s.products += "|" + perImageProductCount;
    s.products += "|" + productPosition;
	s.products=s.products.toLowerCase();
    // set relevant context data    
	s.contextData["shoppingProducts"] = "D=products";
	s.contextData["partner"] = partner;	
	// mention all variables to track
	var contextVars = ['shopping','componentName','componentTitle','partner','products','imageCount','productCount','visibleProductCount','perImageProductCount','productPosition','eventType'];
    s.linkTrackVars = 'products,contextData.shoppingProducts';
    s.linkTrackVars += ',contextData.' + contextVars.join(',contextData.');
    
    // send click beacons
	s.events=null; // make sure this has been cleared
	if(eventType == "impression") {
        // Additional variables set to track custom event
        s.linkTrackVars += ",contextData.eventShoppingProductsImpressions";
        s.contextData["eventShoppingProductsImpressions"] = "1";
        // track prodView, out-of-box event
        s.linkTrackEvents = "prodView";
        s.events = "prodView";
        
		s.tl(this,"o","shopping - products impression");
	}
	else if(eventType == "click") {
        // track scAdd, out-of-box event
		s.linkTrackEvents = "scAdd";
        s.events = "scAdd";        
		s.tl(this,"o","shopping - product click");
        console.log('2021-14-04 shoptrack function fired');
	}
    
    // Clear some of these products-specific variables
	while ( contextVars.length > 0 ) {
		s.contextData[contextVars.pop()] = "";
	}
	s.events="";
	s.products="";
	s.contextData["shoppingProducts"]="";
	s.contextData["partner"]="";
	
    // Probably meant to make sure it doesn't run twice
	sessionStorage.setItem("prodSetByShopTrack", "false");
}

    // old code, but not sure if anything else relies on CQ_Analytics.Sitecatalyst.events
    if (typeof CQ_Analytics === "object" && CQ_Analytics.Sitecatalyst) {
    	CQ_Analytics.Sitecatalyst.events=[];
    }
};

SNI.Analytics.fireGigyaAbandonment = function(event) {
	if ( SNI.Analytics.blockAbandonment ) {
		return;
    }
    
    // probably this block, for CQ_Analytics, should be deleted
	if (typeof CQ_Analytics === "object" && CQ_Analytics.Sitecatalyst) {
		CQ_Analytics.Sitecatalyst.events=[];
    }
    
	if(typeof s === "object"){
        _satellite.logger.log("Tracking Gigya Abandonment");
        s.linkTrackVars = "contextData.eventFormAbandonment,contextData.sweepsFormAbandonment";
        s.contextData["eventFormAbandonment"] = "1";
        s.contextData["sweepsFormAbandonment"] = SNI.Analytics.formGigyaLast;
        s.tl(event, 'o', 'logEvent Gigya abandonment');
        // clear custom event vars
        s.contextData["eventFormAbandonment"] = "";
        s.linkTrackVars = "";
    }
    
    // old, but don't know if needed
	if (typeof CQ_Analytics === "object" && CQ_Analytics.Sitecatalyst) {
		CQ_Analytics.Sitecatalyst.events=[];
    }
};

SNI.Analytics.trackGigyaAbandonment = function(selector) {
	var $form = $(selector);
	if ( $form.length > 0 ) {
		$form.find('input').change(function () {
			SNI.Analytics.formGigyaLast = "last_elememt:"+ $(this).attr('name');
		});
		$form.find('select').change(function () {
			SNI.Analytics.formGigyaLast = "last_elememt:"+ $(this).attr('name');
		});
		$form.submit(function () {
			SNI.Analytics.blockAbandonment = true;
		});
		$(window).bind('beforeunload',function(event){
			SNI.Analytics.fireGigyaAbandonment(event);
		});
    }
};

SNI.Analytics.trackGigyaScreenSet = function(event) {
	var modulename = event.currentScreen;
	if ( modulename === "gigya-register-email-screen" ) {
		SNI.Analytics.trackGigyaAbandonment('.gigya-screen-dialog');
	}
	$('.gigya-screen-dialog div[onclick*=providerClick]').click( function() {
		var $obj = $(this);
		SNI.Analytics.moduleTrackLS(this,{
				ModuleName: modulename,
				LinkTitle: $obj.attr('title'),
				LinkPosition: $('.gigya-screen-dialog div[onclick*=providerClick], a').index($obj),
				TargetUrl: $obj.attr('title') + " Auth Screen"
			});
	});
	$('.gigya-screen-dialog a').click( function() {
		var $obj = $(this);
		if ( $obj.hasClass('gigya-screen-dialog-close') && modulename === "gigya-register-email-screen" ) {
			SNI.Analytics.fireGigyaAbandonment();
		}
		SNI.Analytics.moduleTrackLS(this,{
				ModuleName: modulename,
				LinkTitle: $obj.hasClass('gigya-screen-dialog-close') ? "close" : $obj.html(),
				LinkPosition: $('.gigya-screen-dialog div[onclick*=providerClick], a').index($obj),
				TargetUrl: $obj.attr("data-switch-screen")
			});
	});
}

Consumer Opt-Out Tool, available at <a href="https://optout.networkadvertising.org/?c=1">https://optout.networkadvertising.org/?c=1</a></li>

<li>Connected TV Devices: You can learn more about the choices offered by your TV streaming devices at
<a href="https://www.networkadvertising.org/internet-connected-tv-choices/">https://www.networkadvertising.org/internet-connected-tv-choices/</a></li>
</ul>

<b>Google Opt-Out</b>
<br>
If you are on the web, you can opt out of interest-based Google ads using Google's Ads Settings. Google also participates in the
DAA WebChoices Tool (above).

<br>
<b>Facebook Ad Preferences</b>
<br>
Facebook offers settings that may control what information Facebook uses about you or your device activity for advertising
purposes. Login to Facebook and go to Settings &gt; Ads &gt; Ad Settings (web) or Ad Preferences &gt; Ad Settings (app) for more
information.

your ad blocker or cookie blocker to use these controls.
